CA A 17
2020
Elections: Vote by Mail Ballots
Status: Enacted - Act No. 2019-223
Date of Last Action:*  09/05/2019 - Enacted
Author: Salas (D) Additional Authors: Garcia E (D);Arambula (D);Gonzalez (D)
Topics: Absentee Voting-Misc., Election Crimes, Mail Voting
Summary: Prohibits an employer from requiring or requesting that an employee bring the employee's vote by mail ballot to work or vote the employee's vote by mail ballot at work. Makes a violation of this prohibition subject to a civil fine of up to $10,000 per election.

CA A 49
2020
Voter Protection Act
Status: Enacted - Act No. 2019-553
Date of Last Action:*  10/08/2019 - Enacted
Author: Cervantes (D) Additional Authors: Quirk-Silva (D);Salas (D);Gonzalez (D);Gipson (D);Arambula (D);Gloria (D);Limon (D)
Topics: Absentee Voting-Distributing Ballots, Mail Voting, Polling Places-Locations, Polling Places-Vote Centers
Summary: Requires the elections official to begin mailing vote by mail ballots no later than 29 days before an election and would require that the mailing be complete within 5 days. Prohibits the county elections official from discriminating against any region or precinct in the county in choosing which ballots to mail first within the prescribed 5-day mailing period.

CA A 57
2020
Elections: Names of Candidates
Status: Enacted - Act No. 2019-82
Date of Last Action:*  07/12/2019 - Enacted
Author: Low (D)
Topics: Ballots-Format & Design, Voting Equipment/Technology-Selection & Standards
Summary: Requires that, if a jurisdiction provides a translation of the candidate's alphabet-based names into a character-based language, such as Chinese, Japanese, or Korean, phonetic transliterations of the alphabet-based names of candidate be provided. Requires if a candidate's name is to appear on the ballot in more than one jurisdiction in an election, all of those jurisdictions providing translated ballots and ballot materials to use the same phonetic transliteration or character-based translation of the name.

CA A 59
2020
Elections: Polling Places: University Campuses
Status: Enacted - Act No. 2019-554
Date of Last Action:*  10/08/2019 - Enacted
Author: Kalra (D) Additional Authors: Mullin (D);Cervantes (D);Petrie-Norris (D)
Topics: Polling Places-Locations, Polling Places-Vote Centers
Summary: Directs a county elections official conducting an all-mailed ballot election to consider vote center location on a public or private university or college campus. Expands the definition of ""public building"" for purposes of that provision to include buildings owned or controlled by community college districts, the California State University, and the University of California, and it would also clarify that the University of California is encouraged, but not required, to comply with such a request.

CA S 72
2020
Conditional Voter Registration: Provisional Ballots
Status: Enacted - Act No. 2019-565
Date of Last Action:*  10/08/2019 - Enacted
Author: Umberg (D) Additional Authors: Hertzberg (D);Berman (D);Cervantes (D);Gabriel (D);Gonzalez (D)
Topics: Provisional Voting, Registration-Election Day
Summary: Requires the county elections official to offer conditional voter registration and provisional voting at satellite offices of the County Elections Office and all polling places in that county. Requires the elections official to provide the voter with a ballot for the voter's precinct, if the elections official is able to determine a conditionally registered voter's precinct, and the ballot for that precinct is available. Provides a caveat of certain additional changes.

CA A 100
2020
State Government
Status: Enacted - Act No. 2020-20
Date of Last Action:*  06/29/2020 - Enacted
Author: Budget Cmt
Topics: Cost of Elections
Summary: Establishes the Alfred E. Alquist Seismic Safety Commission as a separate unit within the Office of Emergency Services. Reduces the number of Commissioners and specifies the background qualifications therefor. Includes costs reasonably related to the administration of an election during the coronavirus pandemic as an eligible expenditure that is reimbursable.

CA S 207
2020
Elections: Voter Registration: Partisan Primaries
Status: Enacted - Act No. 2020-01
Date of Last Action:*  02/13/2020 - Enacted
Author: Hurtado (D) Additional Authors: Gonzalez (D)
Topics: Registration-Application Form/Content, Registration-Deadline
Summary: Permits a voter, from a certain number of days immediately preceding an election until the close of polls on election day, in lieu of executing a new affidavit of registration, to change the voter's residence address or political party preference by submitting, to the voter's county elections official, a written request containing the new residence address or political party preference and signed under penalty of perjury.

CA S 288
2020
CEQA: Exemptions: Transportation Related Projects
Status: Enacted - Act No. 2020-200
Date of Last Action:*  09/28/2020 - Enacted
Author: Wiener (D) Additional Authors: Mathis (R);Friedman (D)
Topics: Ballot Access-Candidates, Political Parties
Summary: Relates to the Environmental Quality Act. Exempts from the requirements of CEQA transit prioritization projects, projects by a public transit agency to construct or maintain infrastructure to charge or refuel zero emission transit buses, and projects carried out by a city or county to reduce minimum parking requirements. Requires a lead agency to file a notice of exemption with the Office of Planning and Research and the county clerk of the county in which the project is located.

2020

CA A 3370
2020
Elections Omnibus Bill
Status: Enacted - Act No. 2020-106
Date of Last Action:*  09/18/2020 - Enacted
Author: Elections & Redistricting Cmt
Topics: Candidates-Qualifications for Office, Election Officials-Local, Political Parties
Summary: Amends existing law which prohibits a declaration of candidacy for membership on a county central committee unless the candidate has been affiliated with the political party of that committee for a specified time period. Author: Townsend (D) Additional Authors: Cooke (D);Poore (D);Lynn (D);Matthews (D);Bentz (D);Delcollo (R);Walsh (D);Hansen (D);Chukwuocha (D);Williams K (D);Johnson (D);Minor-Brown (D);Seigfried (D);Walker (D);Brown (D);Lockman (D);Sturgeon (D);Mitchell (D);Ennis (D);McDowell (D);Sokola (D);Cloutier (R);Schwartzkopf (D);Longhurst (D);Brady (D);Kowalko (D);Viola (D);Jaques (D);Johnson S (D);Bolden (D);Heffernan (D);Osienski (D);Baumbach (D);Paradee (D)
Topics: Electoral College-National Popular Vote
Summary: Act enacts the National Popular Vote compact, changes the Electoral College from an institution that reflects the voters state by state choices into a body that reflects the voters nationwide choice, states statutes require that electoral votes are controlled by the plurality of the voters in the state but this system is not required by the U.S. Constitution or federal law.

IL S 1970
2020
Election Code
Status: Enacted - Act No. 624
Date of Last Action:*  01/23/2020 - Enacted
Author: Sims (D) Additional Authors: Collins J (D);Hunter (D);Gabel (D);Morrison (D);Ammons (D);Bennett (D);Murphy L (D);Slaughter (D);Smith (D);Villanueva (D);Belt (D);Villivalam (D);Peters (D);LaPointe (D);Harris G (D)
Topics: Voters-Absence from Work
Summary: Amends the Election Code, provides that a student entitled to vote in a primary, general, or special election or at any election at which propositions are submitted to a popular vote in the state, is entitled to be absent from school to vote on a day in which early voting is offered or on the day of the election, provides that the school may specify the hours in which the student may be absent, provides that a student who is absent from school to vote is not considered absent for the purposes of funding.

2020

Status: Enacted - Act No. 442
Date of Last Action:*  08/21/2019 - Enacted
Author: Aquino (D) Additional Authors: Ammons (D);Williams J (D);Buckner (D);Peters (D);Villivalam (D);Gillespie (D);Belt (D);Tarver (D);Stava-Murray (D);Robinson (D);Villanueva (D);Stuart (D);Greenwood (D);Guzzardi (D);Flowers (D);Welch (D);Fine (D);Mayfield (D);Gabel (D);Lilly (D);Gordon-Booth (D);Ford (D);Hunter (D);Sandoval (D);Martinez (D);Collins J (D);Lightford (D);Harris G (D)
Topics: Absentee Voting-Eligibility, Voters-Felon Voting Rights

ME S 540
2020

Status: Enacted - Act No. 320
Date of Last Action:*  06/17/2019 - Enacted
Author: Luchini (D) Additional Authors: Martin Jo (D);Chipman (D);Gideon (D);Hickman (D);Schneck (D);Farrin (R);Strom (R);Ackley (CSI);Maxmin (D)

Author: Beckett (R)
Topics: Absentee Voting-Misc., Absentee Voting-Returning Ballots, Ballots-Format & Design, Mail Voting
Summary: Provides that absentee ballots received by mail must be postmarked by the date of the election and received by the registrar no more than five business days after the election, conforms to the preceding section, provides that when the deadline for the qualification of candidates has passed or forty five days before the election, whichever is later, the absentee ballots shall be printed on paper of different tints or colors and shall be styled so as to show which ballot is to be used for the first election.

VA H 1
2020
Absentee Voting
Status: Enacted - Act No. 1149
Date of Last Action:*  04/11/2020 - Enacted
Author: Herring (D) Additional Authors: Watts (D);McClellan (D);Tyler (D);McQuinn (D);Kory (D);Keam (D);Filler-Corn (D);Lopez (D);Levine (D);Carter (D);Carroll Foy (D);Gooditis (D);Guzman (D);Willett (D)
Topics: Absentee Voting-No Excuse
Summary: Relates to absentee voting, permits any registered voter to vote by absentee ballot in any election in which he is qualified to vote, removes the current list of statutory reasons under which a person may be entitled to vote by absentee ballot and removes references to those reasons from other sections of the Code.

VA H 43
2020
Provisional Voting
Status: Enacted - Act No. 920
Date of Last Action:*  04/09/2020 - Enacted
Author: Cole (R) Additional Authors: Orrock (R);Sickles (D);Webert M (R);Fowler (R);LaRock (R);Chase (R);Peake (R);Carter (D);Hurst (D);McNamara (R);Cole J (D)
Topics: Counting Votes, Provisional Voting
Summary: Relates to provisional voting, relates to persons voting in split precincts, provides that any voter who is assigned to a precinct that is split between two or more election districts, and who believes he was given a ballot for the district of which he is not a qualified voter, may cast a provisional ballot for the district of which he believes he is a qualified voter and for the district in which the poll book indicates he is registered.

VA H 1103
2020
Ranked Choice Voting
Status: Enacted - Act No. 1054
Date of Last Action:*  04/10/2020 - Enacted
Author: Hudson (D) Additional Authors: Kory (D);Hope (D);Lopez (D);Davis (R);Rasoul (D);Levine (D);Bourne (D);Carter (D);Carroll Foy (D);Guzman (D);Tran (D);Helmer (D);Mugler (D);Subramanyam (D)
Topics: Alt Voting Methods (Ranked Choice, etc)
Summary: Relates to ranked choice voting, provides that elections for local governing bodies may be conducted by ranked choice voting, defines ranked choice voting as the method of casting and tabulating votes in which voters rank candidates in order of preference, tabulation proceeds in rounds in each of which either a candidate or candidates are elected or the last place candidate is defeated, and votes for voters next ranked candidates.
